Not just using it cause they're homophones but the idea of cheaters being people who give very little regard for those they cheat on. They're just meat eaters who get hungry so they go hunting - like a cheetah,ğŸ˜­ And the bite making him a cheetah too was damn clever. That view that people who get cheated on and hurt tend to become the ones who hurt and cheat too.  I loved this move, *2:32*, it looked like it was inspired by Rihanna's super ball performance. I can see the thought behind it though. Cheetahs are known for being fast and so the move looks like paws running, cheetah paws. Great directing from Sean too. Maybe its because he's a dancer too but angle decisions and scenes really complimented the song but didn't drown out the dance. And Jackson, his facial expressions and movements are careless but that really suits the mv. His dancing, however, is still controlled and sharp. Baby I know you have put so much effort into your new music and I know how hard you have worked, so I am concerned that your efforts are not getting the results that should be yours. First of all, I think your team is very inattentive to the release of your music. It used to be that teasers were released constantly a week before the release of a new single, but now it's basically posted on the internet without any teasers. Secondly, the timeline of releasing songs is a bit confusing, first you release the single of "slow", then you release the single and MV of "cheetah", and then you release the MV of "slow" tomorrow, which makes your supporters a bit confused too. Thirdly, my personal thoughts, your perfect looks and rough voice are your unique treasures, I am happy that you are trying a lot of new things, but the current looks and songs are also weakening your strengths to some extent, which I think is a bit of a pity. It's never easy to get music heard by a wider audience, some companies have a whole team to analyze listener preferences, customize numerous beautiful costumes, and promote the music on various platforms. I'm heartbroken that you're fighting almost alone, and I hope you can have a good team to make it all a little easier. Just my personal opinion, I will always love you and support you.

This is my first time listening to a song by Jackson wang and For me "The Cheetah" is a powerful and emotional song that explores the challenges of fame and the struggle to maintain one's identity in the face of intense pressure. The lyrics are evocative and poetic, using imagery of a cheetah running in the dark to convey the sense of vulnerability and isolation that can come with being in the public eye.   The music video is equally impressive, using striking visuals and choreography to convey the song's themes. Jackson Wang's performance is particularly noteworthy, with his movements conveying both strength and vulnerability as he navigates the challenges of fame.   Overall, "The Cheetah" is a compelling and thought-provoking song that offers a nuanced perspective on the experience of being in the public eye. It's a message that is sure to resonate with anyone who has ever felt the weight of expectations bearing down on them, and it's a testament to Jackson Wang's talent as both a musician and a performer.
